 //1 stop flight function
 
 int 1_stop_flight (int choice, char departure_airport[4], char arrival_airport[4])
 {
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4];
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input)
 
     while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
       {
 	if(departure_input==departure_airport)
 	  { 
 	    if(arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 	      {
 	    id=route_id;
 	    printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 	    scanf("%d", &input);
 	    
 	    if(input==1)
 	      {
 		while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 		  {
 		    if(id==route_id)
 		      {
 			while(z<7)
 			  {
 			    if(days[z]==1)
 			      {
 				if(check_days() == TRUE)
 				  {
 				    if(d_letter=='a')
 				      {
 					x=d_hour*60;
 					x=x+d_mins;
 				      }
 				    if(d_letter=='p')
 				      {
 					x=12*60;
 					t=d_hour*60;
 					x=x+t+d_mins;
 				      }
 				  }
 			      }
 			  }
 		      }
 		  }
 	      }
 	    if(input==2)
 	      {
 		while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 		  {
 		    if(id==route_id)
 		      {
 			while(z<7)
 			  {
 			    if(days[z]==2)
 			      {
 				check_days;
 			      }
 			  }
 		      }	     
 		  }
 	      }
 	    if(input==3)
 	      {
 		while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)

 			      }
 			  }
 		      }
 		  }
 	      }
 	    if(input==4)

 		      {

 			  {

 			      {
 				check_days;
 			      }
 			  }	      
 		      }
 		  }
 	      }
 	    if(input==5)
 	      {
 		while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 		  {
 		    if(id==route_id)
 		      {
 			while(z<7)
 			  {
 			    if(days[z]==5)
 			      {
 				check_days;
 			      }
 			  }
 		      }
 		  }
 	      }		
 	    if(input==6)
 	      {
 		while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)

 		      {

 			      {
 				check_days;
 			      }		
 			  }
 		      }
 		  }
 	      }

 	      {
 		while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 		  {
 		    if(id==route_id)
 		      {
 			while(z<7)
 			  {
 			    if(days[z]==7)
 			      {
 				check_days;
 			      }
 			  }
 		      }
 		  }
 	      }
 
 
 	    if(input==0)
 	      {
 		while(fscanf(flights, "%d, %d, (time) (time) (days)", flight_number, route_id, departure_time, arrival_time, (days)) != EOF)
 		  {
 		    if(id==route_id)
 		      {
 			if(*days has daily*)
 			  {
 printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour, a_mins, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);
 			    printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, arrival_city, arrival_state, arrival_input);
 }
 			else
 			  {
 			    printf("Route %s to %s has no 1-stop flights on the specified days\n", departure_input, arrival_input);
 			  }
 		      }
 		  }
 	      }
 	  }
 	else
 	  {
 	    printf("Either airport %s or %s doesn't exist", departure_input, arrival_input);
 	  }

 int 1_stop_flight (int choice, char departure_airport[4], char arrival_airport[4])
 {

       {
 	if(departure_input==departure_airport && arrival_airport != arrival_input)
 	  { 
 	    stop_code=arrival_airport;
 	    while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	      {

 		  {

 		    scanf("%d", &input);

 		      {

 			  {
 			    if(id==route_id)
 			      {

 				  {

 				      {
 					if(check_days() == TRUE)
 					  {
 					    check_time();
 					    if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 					      {
 						printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour, a_mins, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);

 //1 stop flight function
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice, char departure_airport[4], char arrival_airport[4])
 {
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4];
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input)
 
     while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
       {
 	if(departure_input==departure_airport && arrival_airport != arrival_input)
 	  { 
 	    stop_code=arrival_airport;
 	    while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	      {
 		if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 		  {
 		    id=route_id;
 		    printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 		    scanf("%d", &input);
 		    
 		    if(input==1)
 		      {
 			while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 			  {
 			    if(id==route_id)
 			      {
 				while(z<7)
 				  {
 				    if(days[z]==1)
 				      {
 					if(check_days() == TRUE)
 					  {
 					    check_time();
 					    if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 					      {
 						printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour, a_mins, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);
 						printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, arrival_city, arrival_state, arrival_input);
 					      }
 					  }
 				      }
 				  }
 			      }
 			  }
 		      }
 		    if(input==2)
 		      {
 			while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 			  {

 					      }
 					  }

 #include <stdio.h>
 #include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice, char departure_airport[4], char arrival_airport[4])
 {
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4];
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
 
     while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
       {
 	if(departure_input==departure_airport && arrival_airport != arrival_input)
 	  { 
 	    stop_code=arrival_airport;
 	    while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	      {
 		if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 		  {
 		    id=route_id;
 		    printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 		    scanf("%d", &input);
 		    
 		    if(input==1)
 		      {
 			while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c days", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 			  {
 			    if(id==route_id)
 			      {
 				while(z<7)
 				  {
 				    if(days[z]==1)
 				      {
 					if(check_days() == TRUE)
 					  {
 					    check_time();
 					    if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 					      {
 						printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour, a_mins, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);
 						printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, arrival_city, arrival_state, arrival_input);

 #include <stdio.h>
 #include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice, char departure_airport[4], char arrival_airport[4])
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_state[22], departure_city[20], arrival_state[22], arrival_city[20], stop_state[22], stop_city[20], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
 
     while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
       {
 	if(departure_input==departure_airport && arrival_airport != arrival_input)
 	  { 
 	    stop_code=arrival_airport;
 	    while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	      {
 		if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 		  {
 		    id=route_id;
 		    printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 		    scanf("%d", &input);
 		    
 		    if(input==1)
 		      {
 			while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 			  {
 			    if(id==route_id)
 			      {
 				while(z<7)
 				  {
 				    if(days[z]==1)
 				      {
 					if(check_days() == TRUE)
 					  {
 					    check_time();
 					    if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 					      {
 						printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);

 #include <stdio.h>
 #include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice, char departure_airport[4], char arrival_airport[4])
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_state[22], departure_city[20], arrival_state[22], arrival_city[20], stop_state[22], stop_city[20], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10];
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
 
     while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
       {
 	if(departure_input==departure_airport && arrival_airport != arrival_input)
 	  { 
  while(arrival_airport[b] != '\0')  //Renaming the arrays so they can be stored
 		    {
 		      stop_code[b]=arrival_airport[b];
 		      b++;
 		    }
 		  stop_code[b]='\0';
 		  b=0;
 	    while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	      {
 		if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 		  {
 		    id=route_id;
 		    printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 		    scanf("%d", &input);
 		    
 		    if(input==1)
 		      {
 			while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 			  {

 					  {

 					      {

 					      }
 					  }
 				      }
 				  }

 			  }
 		      }

 //"Rebecca Wells"
 //1 stop flight function
 
 #include <stdio.h>
 #include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice, char departure_airport[4], char arrival_airport[4])
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_state[22], departure_city[20], arrival_state[22], arrival_city[20], stop_state[22], stop_city[20], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[20], state[22];
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
 
   while(fscnf(airports, "%s  %s %s", airport_code, city, state) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input==departure_airport && arrival_airport != arrival_input)
 		{ 
 		  while(arrival_airport[b] != '\0')  //Renaming the arrays so they can be stored
 		    {
 		      stop_code[b]=arrival_airport[b];
 		      b++;
 		    }
 		  stop_code[b]='\0';
 		  b=0;
 		  while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 		    {
 		      if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 			{
 			  id=route_id;
 			  printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			  scanf("%d", &input);
 			  
 			  if(input==1)
 			    {
 			      while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				{
 				  if(id==route_id)
 				    {
 				      while(z<7)
 					{
 					  if(days[z]==1)
 					    {
 					      if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						{
 						  check_time();
 						  if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 						    {
 						      printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);
 						      printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, arrival_city, arrival_state, arrival_input);
 						    }
 						}
 					    }
 					}
 				    }
 				}
 			    }
 			  if(input==2)
 			    {
 			      while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				{
 				  if(id==route_id)
 				    {
 				      while(z<7)
 					{
 					  if(days[z]==2)
 					    {
 					      if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						{
 						  check_time();
 						  if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 						    {
 						      printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);
 						      printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, arrival_city, arrival_state, arrival_input);
 						    }
 						}
 					      
 					    }
 					}
 				    }	     
 				}
 			    }
 			  if(input==3)
 			    {
 			      while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)

 #include <stdio.h>
 //#include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_state[22], departure_city[20], arrival_state[22], arrival_city[20], stop_state[22], stop_city[20], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[20], state[22], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4];
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscnf(airports, "%s  %s %s", airport_code, city, state) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input==departure_airport && arrival_airport != arrival_input)
 		{ 
 		  while(arrival_airport[b] != '\0')  //Renaming the arrays so they can be stored
 		    {
 		      stop_code[b]=arrival_airport[b];
 		      b++;
 		    }
 		  stop_code[b]='\0';
 		  b=0;
 		  while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 		    {
 		      if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 			{
 			  id=route_id;
 			  printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			  scanf("%d", &input);
 			  
 			  if(input==1)
 			    {
 			      while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				{
 				  if(id==route_id)
 				    {
 				      while(z<7)
 					{
 					  if(days[z]==1)
 					    {
 					      if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						{
 						  check_time();
 						  if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 						    {
 						      printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, departure_city, departure_state, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code);
 						      printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, stop_city, stop_state, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, arrival_city, arrival_state, arrival_input);
 						    }
 						}
 					    }
 					}
 				    }
 				}
 			    }

 			    {

 //1 stop flight function
 
 #include <stdio.h>
 //#include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4];
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscnf(airports, "%s  %s %s", airport_code, city, state) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])

 {

   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");

 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");

     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])

 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);

 						    {
 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);

 //1 stop flight function
 
 #include <stdio.h>
 #include <string.h>
 //#include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscnf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);
     
 		      while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 			{
 			  if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 			    {
 			      id=route_id;
 			      printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			      scanf("%d", &input);
 			      
 			      if(input==1)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==1)
 						{
 						  //if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);
 							}
 						    }
 						}
 					    }
 					}
 				    }
 				}
 			      if(input==2)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==2)
 						{
 						  if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {

 //1 stop flight function
 
 #include <stdio.h>
 #include <string.h>
 //#include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);
     
 		      while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 			{
 			  if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 			    {
 			      id=route_id;
 			      printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			      scanf("%d", &input);
 			      
 			      if(input==1)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==1)
 						{
 						  //if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);
 							}
 						    }
 						}
 					    }
 					}
 				    }
 				}
 			      if(input==2)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==2)
 						{
 						  //if(check_days() == TRUE)

 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)

 //1 stop flight function
 
 #include <stdio.h>
 //#include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);
     
 		      while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 			{
 			  if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 			    {
 			      id=route_id;
 			      printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			      scanf("%d", &input);
 			      
 			      if(input==1)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==1)
 						{
 						  //if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);
 							}
 						    }
 						}
 					    }
 					}
 				    }
 				}
 			      if(input==2)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==2)
 						{
 						 // if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);
 							}
 						    }  
 						}

 //"Rebecca Wells"
 //1 stop flight function
 
 #include <stdio.h>
 #include <string.h>
 //#include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);
 		      rewind(routes);
 		      while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 			{
 			  if(stop_code==departure_airport && arrival_input==arrival_airport)
 			    {
 			      id=route_id;
 			      printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			      scanf("%d", &input);
 			      
 			      if(input==1)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==1)
 						{
 						  //if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);
 							}
 						    }
 						}
 					    }
 					}
 				    }
 				}
 			      if(input==2)
 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==2)
 						{
 						 // if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);

   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);
 		      rewind(routes);

   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)   //scan for the departure code but not to the arrival code
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)  //finds the name of the city of the departure airport
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    {

 		      rewind(routes);
 		      while(fscanf(routes, "%d  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)  //now searches for the place where the stop is the 
 			{                                                                                      //depart airport and the arrival input is correct
 			  if(stop_code[0]==departure_airport[0] && stop_code[1]==departure_airport[1] && stop_code[2]==departure_airport[2] && arrival_input[0]==arrival_airport[0] && arrival_input[1]==arrival_airport[1] && arrival_input[2]==arrival_airport[2])
 			    {
 			      id=route_id;
 			      printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			      scanf("%d", &input);
 			      
 			      //now depending on the day entered, program is suppose to run through each option that was entered, find where the id is similar, then
 			      //check the days, finally check the time that is involved in the stop to make sure the layover is the correct time
 			      //end with printing out the message if you find a suitable one stop flight

 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==1)
 						{
 						  //if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      // check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);
 							}
 						    }
 						}
 					    }
 					}
 				    }
 				}

 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;

   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)   //scan for the departure code but not to the arrival code
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)  //finds the name of the city of the departure airport
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])

 #include <stdio.h>
 #include <string.h>
 //#include "airports.h"
 
 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)   //scan for the departure code but not to the arrival code
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)  //finds the name of the city of the departure airport
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);
 		      rewind(routes);
 		      departure_airport[0]="";
 		      departure_airport[1]="";

 		      arrival_airport[1]="";
 		      arrival_airport[2]="";

 			{                                                                                      //depart airport and the arrival input is correct
 			  if(stop_code[0]==departure_airport[0] && stop_code[1]==departure_airport[1] && stop_code[2]==departure_airport[2] && arrival_input[0]==arrival_airport[0] && arrival_input[1]==arrival_airport[1] && arrival_input[2]==arrival_airport[2])
 			    {
 			      id=route_id;
 			      printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");
 			      scanf("%d", &input);
 			      
 			      //now depending on the day entered, program is suppose to run through each option that was entered, find where the id is similar, then
 			      //check the days, finally check the time that is involved in the stop to make sure the layover is the correct time

 				{
 				  while(fscanf(flights, "%d %d %d:%d%c %d:%d%c %s", flight_number, route_id, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, days) != EOF)
 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)
 					{
 					  while(z<7)
 					    {
 					      if(days[z]==1)
 						{
 						  //if(check_days() == TRUE)
 						    {
 						      // check_time();
 						      if(layover >= 60 && layover <= 120)
 							{
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, travel_days, d_hour, d_mins, d_letter, departure_city, departure_input, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, a_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code);
 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);

 //1 stop flight function
 
 #include <stdio.h>

 int one_stop_flight(int choice)
 {
   int route_id, id, input, flight_number, d_hour, d_mins, a_hour, a_mins, d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, a_hour_stop, a_mins_stop, z, layover, b;
   char departure_input[4], arrival_input[4], stop_code[4], days[7], departure_city[50], arrival_city[50], stop_city[50], arrival_time[7], departure_time[7], a_letter, d_letter, travel_days[10], airport_code[4], city[50], arrival_airport[4], departure_airport[4], a_letter_stop, d_letter_stop;
   FILE *airports, *flights, *routes;
 
   printf("Enter departure and arrival airport codes: ");
   scanf("%s %s", departure_input, arrival_input);
   flights = fopen("flights.txt", "r");
   airports = fopen("airports.txt", "r");
   routes = fopen("routes.txt", "r");
 
   while(fscanf(airports, "%s  %50[^\n]", airport_code, city) != EOF)   //scan for the departure code but not to the arrival code
     {
       if(airport_code != departure_input || airport_code != arrival_input)
 	{
 	  while(fscanf(routes, "%d.  %s %s", &route_id, departure_airport, arrival_airport) != EOF)  //finds the name of the city of the departure airport
 	    {
 	      if(departure_input[0]==departure_airport[0] && departure_input[1]==departure_airport[1] && departure_input[2]==departure_airport[2])
 		{
 		  if(arrival_airport[0] != arrival_input[0] || arrival_airport[1] != arrival_input[1] || arrival_airport[2] != arrival_input[2])
 		    { 
 		      strcpy(stop_code, arrival_airport);
 		      rewind(routes);
 		      departure_airport[0]=' ';
 		      departure_airport[1]=' ';

 			{                                                                                      //depart airport and the arrival input is correct
 			  if(stop_code[0]==departure_airport[0] && stop_code[1]==departure_airport[1] && stop_code[2]==departure_airport[2] && arrival_input[0]==arrival_airport[0] && arrival_input[1]==arrival_airport[1] && arrival_input[2]==arrival_airport[2])
 			    {
 			      id=route_id;
 			      printf("Enter a day of the week (1-7, or 0 for all days):");

 				    {
 				      if(id==route_id)

 							  printf("Flight %d (%s)\n    %d:%d.m. %s, %s (%s)\n    %d:%d%c.m. %s (%s)\n", flight_number, (days), d_hour_stop, d_mins_stop, d_letter_stop, stop_city, stop_code, a_hour, a_mins, a_letter, arrival_city, arrival_input);
